Ngusuku lokuphela kwenyanga namhlanje. Injalo nje iphela iqophisana neviki. Kuyaphithizela lapha Kwa. MaNkabinde. Kukhona yonke inhlobo yabantu. Ku. khona wenasifazane wenamlisa inqobo nje yikuthi nxa kuyinkolotshe. Babodwa abaxexebuka isikhumba se. buze kuvele esilanda esomlungu. Babodwa abamilomo 
isiyaba bomvu. Kukhona abamehlo asahlala ekhala igazi. Abanye bana. maqhushelana ezisu ezingamapaklaklana wena wabona amatshwele ezi. nkukhu achamiselwe ngomshini; kungasabanga yinto efana nezisu eziva. misa ukubonakala ezimakwini ezizitholela amakhaya emizini okusuke kuhlatshiwe kuyo ngenxa yendlala yasemakubo - zihilele zihilele zihle' zikhuluphale ngezisu. 
  Naphezu kokuba sekuphithizela kanje, yilokhu besangena abanye. Ku. ngena abanezingozingozi, kungene abazibazibazi kungene abamsulwa, abesulekile kahle abangakaqoqodi ekubeni ngamabutho alapha ekhaya. 'Bayamangalisa abaningi besifazane abagcwele lapha. Nxa ubheka isitho sakhona usibona sesaba nezihluzu' sakhipha amajaqamba; kungenjalo ziba yimicondo emnyama. Abangasifaki isicathulo noma ihliphasi ubona ingqa. 
. kala esiyajika umbala yaba mnyama. Abanye sebephuphuzela uboya ebu. sweni sebephenduke amahwanqa ezifunda. Babodwa ababhema usikilidi, babodwa abagoqa imboza ifakazela ibhulukwe, eligqokiwe phela. 
  Uyasha usikilidi. Imile injomu noma isikali sembamba lapha phambi kwabo. Nxa esiphakamisa lowo ophuzayo uqale asinyakazise ayiyakaze. Akuvamisi ukuthi kube yidlanzana lamadoda odwa. Uthola kukhona oyedwa noma ababili besimame bephuzisana nawo amadoda lawo. Nxa ubabuka uqaphelisise ubuso babo laba odade uthola ukuthi izinyama zabo ziyashwileka zisonteke. Azishwabani njengezinyama zabantu asebekhulile zenze imixhiliba. Into efika idunge ingqondo nomcabango kumuntu onge. jwayele ukuhlangabezana nesimo esinjena yimpilo ephilwa yilaba odade. 8 

Nxa umi ubheke eMpumalanga ukwaMaNkabinde, weqa imizi elisonto ngokwenyukela ngesandla sokhohlo. Umuzi olandela lowo kukwaDolothiya. Akusiwona umuzi onokubabazeka okuthize nxa kukhulunywa ngesakhiwo. Isakhiwo sakhona sikhulu nokho siluhlobo Iwesilungu. 

Yilapho kuqalela khona isigoai sase-Antiyokhi, kulomuzi. UDolothiya lona kwabe kuyintombi eyayingazange igane. 
Yonke imihla yokuphila kwakhe wabe eyichithe eyisisebenzi sakwaDokotela u Varendhoff. lodokotela wayesuke naye eThekwlini weza naye eFiIidi. Ngezinsuku ayefike ngazo eFilidi wayesevele ekhulile. Q. 
  Wangena-ke emsebenzini uMshini umfo kaNgcobo. Waba nekhono elihle, wakhuthala. Ukusebenza kwakhe kwamenza wavuleka ingqondo. Walubona usizi ayefikele kula emhlabeni. Wayifunda yonke imisebenzi yalapha ehhotela. Yayikhona indawo yokulala izisebenzi. Kwakuyaye kuthi nxa eshayisa ebusuku emsebenzini ala Ie khona, kodwa nxa eshayisa emini wayehamba aye ekhaya e-Antiyokhi. 
  Ububi buyahambelana nobuhle lapha ezweni. Ububi bubonakala ubukhona babo nxa buqhathaniswa nalokho okuthiwa kuhle. Kanjalo futhi nakumntwana ezelwe uya nokuya enza izinto ezincomekayo, ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kube sekuba khona amabadlana amabi kuhle kwenhlava ingenela ikhaba lilihle lichachambile. Okuvamisa ukuba lukhuni kakhulu yikuthi nxa izinto ezimbi zivelela umuntu ziza zelakanyane noma zenanelane. 

UDolothiya wayesekhulile, namehlo akhe ayeseqala ukuba luvindi. "Mntanomnewethu, ilanga seliyashona. Noyihlo ngamgcina wena ungakazalwa eyilokhu ehla enyuka nemikhumbi olwandle. Angisenalo nethemba lokuthi ngabe usawadla yini anhlamvana, noma sewadliwa yizinhlanzi. Wowu! Ngiyazisa ngomntakababa." 

  Wathula umfana ezwa indaba eyayiyinkinga, ezindlebeni nasemqo-. ndweni. Wayezazi engenayise, engenanina. UDolothiya wayeyikho konke kuye. Ayikho into ayengayibuza, ayikho futhi into ayengayisho. Waqhubeka uyisekazi. 
  "Ubudoda abukhulelwa. Ngingeke ngithi usemncane kangangokuthi ungeke wazithathela intombi uganwe. Izifiso zami yikuthi nxa ngihamba lapha emhlabeni, ngikushiye usuzinzile uganiwe. Ngalokhokwenza uzobe uzibekela esinye sezisekelo zempilo nenkambo yalapha ezweni. Uyobe uzenzela inqaba nesiphephelo sakho, uzitholela umfowenu ukuze ungasali ufana nohlanga lusele lulodwa ensimini, ungafani nempundle isihlahla esesiphundleke onke amagatsha namahlamvu aso. Angifisi ukuba uzwe usizi lokuba nguyedwana, ngoba lukhulu kabi. Nxa uyindoda engenamfazi, awuhlukene nefa Iikamdliwayini; uphangwa uze uphangwe nangabantu abayiziwula kunawe, abangenabo ubuhlakani obungase bube nomfutho ongakukhinyabeza uwele ezandleni zabo. Indlela oweza ngayo emhlabeni ulethwa nguyihlo nonyoko, angifisi ukuthi nawe ulethe izingane ngayo. Angithandi futhi ukuyixoxa ngoba nokusinda kwakho, ufike ubekwe ezandleni zami; ungashuthekwa emapayipini kumbe ulahlwe emigqonyeni yezibi yaseThekwini, nami ngikwamukele ngikukhulise, kuyizimangaliso zikaThixo. Yonke into yalapha emhlabeni iyizinsizi. Injabulo yakhona iphuma ezinsizini, idale izinsizi nxa lowomuntu eqondene nave ethi uyayetshisa. Angingakubambezeli, funa uze ushiywe yisikhathi somsebenzi. Hamba nalamagama engikunika wona: Thatha, uganwe uzakhele umuzi, ngoba ubucu obuhle buhamba ngabubili."

ngengane eyizele na? Yena uyise?

Nxa umphupha lomuntu akhulume nawe akuyaleze ngezinto ezithile, uthi nxa uthi ufuna ukubonana naye ubuso nobuso umthole esebanda kodwa engakembelwa, lento ifika yambule ubunzulu obuthize_obusebuqinisweni bengqikithi yokuphila.   Umuntu nomuntu uyaye azibone eyisihlakaniphi esikhulu nxa ephethe imali abangayiphethe abanye. UJuly wayeyilokhu elindele uNonsizi ukuthi abuye. Lalibuye lithi nto

59  

UNqobile wayeyohlanganisa umnyaka weshumi athatha isibopho sokuba yinkosikazi yomuzi wayo. Uthando Iwabo noNgcobo Iwabe selukhulile; lusakhula futhi ludlondlobala. Izingane zazimbili, ekhulelwe eyesithathu. Kwakungumfana wamazibulo uSibusiso elanywa yintombazanyana uSilomo. 
  Ngalezizinsuku uNqobile wayethi nxa embuka uNgcobo umyeni wakhe noyise wabantabakhe azibone emusha egcwele amandla afana nawomqumbe ufutha uvulela imbali ukuba iqhakaze. Wayezizwa emzimbeni sengathi uyancencetha kuhle kwezinsimbi zamasonto ezikhala ziyozwakala ezinzulwini zenhliziyo zithinte imizwa ehambisanayo nengahambisani nesonto. UNgcobo wayeyisibuko eyayizibuka kuso intokazi kaSishi. Yilapho eyayibona khona ubuntombi bayo nokugcwala kwabo. Kwakuyima ebona sengathi uthando Iwabo luselusha. 
  Nokhoke ngemva kwaleminyaka, sebenekhanya elifudumele ubukhosikazi babugcwele nswi kuNqobile. NoNgcobo wabe ondlekile, egcwele ukukhanga okufana nokwesithombo esigcwele ubusha sizifikisela ngehlobo elinezimvula, nentokomalo nemvundo. Izinwele zakhe zazimnyama kuhle kwamahlungu abatshelwe kuthangi kwalandela izihlambi zageza umlotha asala engasenantuthu yamadaka namungu. 
  Namhlanje kuphela izinsuku ezihlanganisa amasonto amabili uNgcobo engasaziwa ekhaya. Yinto evamisile ukuthi ngezinye izinsuku ake angabuyi ekhaya. Nokho-ke noma kunjalo azikaze zelamane zize zihlanganise isonto. Njengoba esemabili nje sekukukhulu kudlula ukwenza. Kusasa kuyogonywa izingane. UNqobile kufuneka athathe uSilomo ayomgoma. Ngenxa yokuthi kanamuntu azomshiya ekhaya kufanele asheshe ahambe ukuze nave abe kanye namafolosi. 
  Nangempela wavuka ngomuso walungisela uSibusiso wamhloma indlela ebheke esikoleni. Waqeda lapho wathatha uSilomo waqonda nave eLuthela. Ababeqondene nomsebenzi wokugonywa kwenzingane babehlele ukuthi lezongane ezifunda isikole zigonyelwe ezikoleni. 
  Wafika eLuthela bengakabi baningi abazali, nezingane. Wafika isekhona nendawo yokuthi ahlale phansi aphumule. Wafike wahlala eduze komunye umakoti owayengaba butholinye nave. Lomakoti wayelethe okuyinganyana yentombazane. Babingelelana nalomakoti, bathol ana ngomoya. Nezingane zabo ngakolunye uhlangothi zazitholana. Lona kwabe kungumakoti wesisebenzi sezenhlalakahle uSibeko. 
  Ngesikhathi bexoxa baze bafika ekuthini baqhathanise ubudala bezingane zabo. Kwabakhanyela ngokwezibalo ukuthi uSiiomo noMesuli bayalingana bashiyana ngezinyanga. Babedlala oSilomo no Mesuli, benganake lutho, wena owabona inkonyane itshekula yesuthi ubisi lukanina.

Wathola ingane yomfana wayinika igama lokuthi ngu5ikhumbuzo. Ngemva kwezinsuku ezinhlanu ekhululekile isibhedlela samkhipha wabuyela emzini wakhe. 

  Ekufikeni kwakhe ekhaya wafikela phezu kwayo leyo nsumansumane ayeyishiyile; insumansumane yokulahleka komuntu emdala, engenkomo yona eke iduke, engengane yona eke iduke, engeyona nemali yona eke ibhoboze imbobo ekhukhwini iziwele lapho eziqathakela khona. 

  Wafika umhlobo wakhe ezombona. Wayephethe izipho zokukhunga mgane, emphathele nesheke elaliyinkokhelo yakhe ngesandla ayekade esifake mhla kugonywa izin'gane. Bahlala bexoxa bejabule baze behlukana, lutho ukuyithinta eyokunyamalala kukaNgcobo. Nazi izinsuku zemikhosi yokhisimusi nonyaka omusha zisondela, kodwa uNgeobo kasondeli. Nazi ziqhela ziqhela naye. 66 

  Wasukuma uSibeko waphuma waya kwaMaNkabinde. Wasala ekhala uThandiwe waze wayozishaya phansi walala. 
  Ukuhamba kuzala induna. Lomntanabantu wayezisukele eMgungundlovu eza nomyeni wakhe eFilidi kanti kabuzanga elangeni. Nali iFilidi selimdala imfilidi, ubhelebana uqobo. Lesisimo esingesihle nempilo yoganano Iwabo eyabe isingenwa yinhlava akubanga yinto ebuyayo. Kwaba yinto eqhubekayo. Kukhona into eyisimangaliso eyenziwa ngabantu kwabanye abantu lapha phansi komthunzi welanga. Nxa uke uqaphele uyoyibona kumuntu nxa egibele ibhayisikili kungelona elakhe kumbe imoto. Ulifaka ezikhwesheni alibophe kushunqe uthuli elikhokhoza ngoba engalithandi. Kakhombisi ukuthi unalo uzwelo ngesithukuthuku esaconsa lisetshenzelwa. Vinto enjena lena oyaye uzwe kuthiwa kukhona ukuxhaphaza. 

  Kwakuyiso lesi-ke nakuSibeko. UStutu wayazi ukuthi uSibeko kayena owakhe, ungokaMaNtuli. Wamxhaphaza, yebuya kumxhaphaza. Wayemsinisa kuhle kukanodoli. Siye sizwe abantu bethi kukhona igobondela. Lidumile igobondela. Abalaziyo indlela elisebenza ngayo bathi umuntu ofakwe lona ugila imikhuba emangalisayo, indoda iphenduke isiyoyoyo. Asazi-ke noma noSibeko labe selimngene yini igobondela. Noma singazi kodwa iqiniso liyikuthi nxa igobondela Iiyenzisa amahlazo indoda, ilahlekelwe yisithunzi, lowomfazi osuke eyifake lona usuke enze ngoba kungeyona eyakhe, engenalo uthando Iwayo, kodwa ona ehlikizela labo abaqondene nayo. 

  Kwahamba kwahamba uSibeko wabonakala engayile emsebenzini ehleli kwaMaNkabinde, emzini wesikokiyana. Kwala kuMaNtuli nxa sekunje. Wageina wamkhulumisa ngalesisenzo esibi kanje. Lokhukumsola kwakhe kwahle kwabeka obala ukuthi uyinyathele emsileni kuStutu. Kwabe sekukhona izaga ezigigiyelayo ebizwa ngento ezala izibhueu, kuthiwe kabuke izindandatho lezo eyamfaka zona indoda, wayeyebile kungeyona eyakhe. Onke lamagama ayephuma emaseleni oqobo, amasela akwazi ukweba umphefumulo. 
  USibeko wayengasengabungabu ukubuya eze emzini wakhe. Nesandla sa be sesiqala ukuthi sibe lukhuni angakhiphi izimfanelo ngokufanele. Ngolunye usuku wabuya weza kwakhe. Wathi esahleli kwabe sekuthunyelwa isigijimi sizombiza. Kazange asukumele phezulu'"'Umphumela walokho kwaba yikuthi afike yen a mathupha uStutu esezomkhipha. Kwathi nxa behambile wathula uThandiwe. Wahlala wahlala ethule wayesedumela isibuko wazibuka. Wezwakala ephubuka ehleka yedwa ethi: "Cha kodwa umuhle mntakaNtuli, uhlanzekile futhi. Ungakhiphi into ebolile ngomlomo wakho. Okubolile wakuzala kodwa usunokuphilayo."

  "Mathenjwa, nginike isithuba ngiphefumule, ngemva kwalokho ngizobe sengigonyuluka. Indawo yokulala nalolutho engilukhwixelise emhlane wami, anginayo.   UMaNtuli wayephethe ibhokisanyana okwakubonakala ukuthi lifakwe emsebenzini elabe Iingawulungiselwe. Kulelibhokisanyana, elabe Iilibhokisanyana ngokuguga elabe liyikho hayi ngobuncane, wayefake ukudla kwakhe kanye nebhodlela likaphalafini nezinye izintwanyana ayengase azidinge, kuhle kwekhabethe elinesiphambano esibomvu losizo lokuqala. 
  Wayethula ingane wayoyilalisa kwezinye. Ngemva kwalokhu wabasa isitofu sikaphalafini wabeka amanzi okwenza itiye ukuba baphunge bazibe namakhaza. Ngesikhathi amanzi esafudumala waqalela wamkhininde/a inkinga yempilo nenhlalo yakhe nomfo kaSibeko. Afudumala amanzi, abila, bawathatha, babe sebephunga. Itiye ababeliphunga lalingakapheli ngesikhathi kwehla izinyembezi emehlweni abo bobabili. Lake lema phakathi naphakathi ezinkomishini, zehla izinyembezi zibuye ziconsele kulo. 

  Lesisigameko sasiyisithombe esiluvindi ngempi/o yalapha ezweni. Itiye babengalifakanga usawoti, babelifake ushukela yikuphela, kanti konke okulapha emhlabeni kumnandi ngendlela yakho. Okubabayo kumnandi ngokubaba kwakho, kodwa kukhona izinga okufika kulo kungabe kusehla emphinjeni. Nxa umuntu eqe kulologibe Iwalelozinga, okuningi okuthunaza ubumtoti bokuphila, kuyanyobozela kube namahloni kungabe kusathanda ukujwayela eduze kwakhe. Lelijwayezi e/iyikuqhela kwesitha, lidalwa yisibindi, ukuzinikela, ithemba lesinxephezelo esiyinzuzo, nokukholwa okungagudluki; konke okuyizikhali ezidingwa ngumphili-mpilo ukuba azididiyele ndawonye athake insizi yezinsizi. Yingakho-ke ekukhulumeni kwakwaZulu kukhona isaga esithi ukuphuza inyongo.

UNqobile wayengakuthandisisi ukuba nomuntu oyisiqashi kwakhe. Ezinsukwini uNgcobo engakanyamalali wayeke wazama kaningi uNgcobo ukuxoxa naye ekhulumela abantu ababefuna ukuthi baqashe ikamelo. Wenqaba waphetha oKaMathenjwa. Ziningike izizathu ezazidala ukuthi enqabe. Wayezichaza futhi. 

  Nxa ungumuntu osakhulisa abantwana ubafundisa eyakho imfundiso, akukuhle ukuba nesiqashi. Isiqashi siba neyaso imfundiso kwezaso izingane engeke ize ifane neyakho kwezakho. Esinye sifika singenazo izingane sibe sesikwemuka ezakho. Nxa sidla umaconsana noma yisikokiyana noma yimbamba, ngelinye ilanga sigcina sesithuma izingane zakho ziyosithengela. Okudlulela kakhulu yikuthi siqhamuka sesifundisa izingane ukuthi nxa zikade zithunyiwe kuhle zihole, sithume ingane esitolo iyabuya siyinika amasenti. Leyongane ayisenakubuye ibe ngeyakho, futhi ayisekubuye iwuzwe umthetho wakho ngoba awuyiniki amasenti nxa ukade uyithume esitolo. 

  Wayezithanda izingane zakhe oKa5ishi. Wayezithanda ngaphezulu kukayise wazo. Lokhoke kuyinto evamile ukuthi nxa unesithombe somuntu omthandayo ungadeli yikuzibukela sona, kodwa nxa ubone yena luqobo Iwakhe kukusinde ukumbuka. Kafuphi zaziyisithombe sikaNgcobo, zingumlando wenkambo nempilo kayise nonina. Inkomazi nxa izala iyaqopha ophondweni, nazoke zaziyiwo amazenga kuNqobile, ziyizithelo zobusha nokukhula kwakhe . 

  Kwasekuntwela ezansi ngenkathi u5ikhumbuzo eklabalasa ekhala. Kwakuyisongathi ukhumbuza onina ukuthi izinyoni sezivukile ukuyophandela amaphuphu azo. Baphaphama benza umkhuleko wokusa. Kwathi nxa beqedile uNqobile wancelisa u5ikhumbuzo. Ngalenkathi uThandiwe wayempompa isitofu epheka amanzi okuhlamba nokwenza itiye. Athi ukuba abile wayesenza itiye. Waqeda ukwenza itiye wathelela izingane awokuhlamba, zahlamba u5ibusiso walungela indlela yesikole. 

  Waphindela ebhokisini lakhe (Iosizo 10kuqa,la) wakhipha isinkwa nephehlwa (ibhotela). Wasisika izingcezu wathelela"izingane itiye wazipha. Ngemva kwalokhu kwaba yima elungisa owabo noNqobile umkhumiso. Zaqala izingane zakhombisa ukujabula sezesuthi. Nonina bazizwa bethola umfutho omusha nethemba elikhulayo. Zazidlala ekhishini izithandani 05ilomo noMesuli.

  Lesisenzo samdidaingqondo uMaNtuli, ikakhulukazi ngoba wayeqala ukuba aze ahlangabezane noNqobile ekulesisimo. Ukuphikisana kwakudlangile lapha kwaBhanya. Umkhankaso wokuzakha nokuzenzela wawumkhulu. Kwabe sekuphele iminyaka emibili inkosazana emhlophe eyabivela phesheya kwezilwandle iwuzama lomsebenzi. UNkosazana Nash wayeqale wakhinyabezwa yikuthi ulimi IwesiZulu wayengalwazi. Nokho-ke ngomoya ayenawo nenhloso yakhe umsebenzi wawuqhubeqhubeka. UNkosazana Nash wayesenawo amalungu ambalwa ayesewatholele inhlangano yabesifazane eyayinomgomo wokuzakha nokuzenzela. Nokho wayesayilokhu eqhubekile nokugalaja. Laligijima njalo ibhayisikili lakhe. Wayevamisile ukudlula ngakwaNgcobo, kusukela ezinsukwini uNqobile engakahlali noThandiwe. Nokho-ke wayedlula ngaphandle angangeni. 
  Ngelinye i1anga wedlula bephezu kwawo umsebenzi wokulungisa ingadi. Indlela ababesebenza ngayo yamkhanga wabe esezinikela ekuthini axoxe nabo. Waphenduka wabuya ngebhayisikili lakhe. Wema ngaphandle kothango wababingelela. Bavuma. Wabe esekhuluma ngolimi IwesiLungu wathi: 
"Ngiyayilhanda lento eniyenzayo. Ngingeza yini ngizonincedisa na?" Basebeya ekuwuphetheni umsebenzi wabo nokho bamemukela. Wabe esejikela ngasesangweni bamhlangabeza. Bamvulela isango wangenisa ibhayisikili lakhe waleyamisa endlini ngaphansi komthunzi. 
  "Ngicela ukuphinda nginibingelele futhi. Mina isibongo sami nginguNash. Igama ngingu Carol. Ngivamisile njalo ukunidlula nenza lomsebenzi wengadi, njengoba namhlanje sengize ngithi angizonisiza. Ngingumgqugquzeli wenhlangano yabesimame abazama ukuzakha nokuzenzela. Lokhu enikwenzayo ngiyakuthanda futhi kungolunye Iwezinhlelo ezingaphansi komgomo wenhlangano yami." Wayekhuluma uNkosazana Nash, ekhuluma nje, esephezu komsebenzi encedisa lamakhosikazi. 
  Wabe esesuka uNqobile eyohlola amanzi endlini ababesawabasele benzela ukufudumeza ilhumbu. Basala oThandiwe noCarol Nash beqedela umsebenzi. Wawafica esebila amanzi uNqobile wabe esenza iliye walungisa namakomishi. Wathi ukuba aqede wayesebabizela endlini. Wabanika amanzi bahlamba izandla, babe sebekhuluma nazo izinkomishi. UNkosazana Nash wancoma ukuhlangana nabantu akwazi ukukhuluma nabo ngolimi Iwakhe bezwane. Waphakamisa ukukhululeka komphefumulo wakhe nxa ethola ukwamukeleka ngendlela abamemukela ngayo. Wayengavamisi ukutholana nabantu abazi izilimi zesiLungu. Nabo, ngakolwabo uhlangothi, babesamangele besadidekile yikuthi mihlola mini lena ebavelelayo. Nokho-ke ngalokhokuhlangana kwangalowomzuzu, babe sebudaleka ubungane nobudlelwane.

isikhwama sakhe wabakhiphela izigqebhezana ezabe zilotshwe igama lakhe nekheli lamahhovisi akhe kanye negama lenhlangano yakhe. Wabatshela ukuthi uyophinda abavakashele ngesonto elilandelayo. Umehluko lapha uba yikuthi umuntu osiza abanye nxa kukhona amncedile uyajabula, ahlumeleleke amandla akhe, akhule ezifisweni ezinhle nasekuzotheni. Wonke umndeni wawusuyifundile 'Insizi yezinsizi' ngaphandle kukaSikhumbuzo. Bahlabelela yona. Bathi bangayiqeda kwabe sekuphakwa ukudla kwakusihlwa. 
Ngesikhathi sekulungile ukudla bahlabelela iculo lokubonga: 

"Lokhukudl' esikudlayo Sikuphiwa nguwe Nalamanzi 'siwaphuzayo Siwaphiwa Nguwe." 
  Babezifundisa bezikhulisa ngayo yonke imfundiso enhle. Abanye abantu bayaye bakhohlwe yikuthi ukubonga kuyinto enkulu kabi. Ayikho indlela yokucela eyedlula ukuthi ubonge. Nxa ubonga ngamanye amazwi usuke ucelela ingomuso. Nxa umuntu umupha, engabongi usuke eqonde ukuthi lokho omuphe khona ubengakuncengile. Kuvamisile ukuthi nxa inala isinkulu ukubonga kukhohlakele. Ngenxa yemilomo ehlulwa yigama elinamalunga amane nje: Ngi-ya-bo-nga indlala iya nokwanda, ,nokuncipha kwezinto ezinhle kuyanda. Ukungeneliswa kuyanda, okuyinzalo yomhawu odalwa yikuzazi kokuthi mina, umuntu akhohlwe yikuthi unguBhekukuphiwa ikati lasehotela. 110 

UNgcobo wayesejubalele, beyilokhu bengamazanga abantabakhe. Lalingasekho ngisho iphunga lakhe eFilidi. Wayezihlalele eDumbe enza wona umsebenzi wamahotela. Lapha eDumbe wayaziwa ngegama lokuthi nguSihlobo. Abanye babethi nguSihlobosengane. Babebodwa ababethi unguSihlobesihle. Umumo wakhona leligama abametha lona babeqonde ukuthi uyisihlobo esedukelene nezihlobo zaso. Kuyinto okumelwe ukuthi noma nini ingakhohlakali ukuthi okubolile kuvela kokuphilayo. Yingakho abadala bethi umphanda ubulawa yizakhelani uphinde ubezwe bethi isitha somuntu ngabendlu yakhe. Izihlubuki zivama ukuba ngabantu abasuke bekade bethembekile. Nomfo kaNgcobo wayengumuntu owayengeke asolakalela ekuthini angaphenduka gwiqiqi abe esethunjwa liDumbe adele wonke umnotho wakhe owawungumuzi nezingane nayo yonke insebenzo yamandla obusha bakhe, konke okwakubekelelwe kwaBhanya. 
  Yinto evamisa ukudida ingqondo ukuthi yini into edala ukuthi umuntu wesilisa nxa ekhula engcebeni nasemnothweni abe esebona ukuthi kuhle aqoqe sonke isifazane somhlaba sibe ngesakhe. Ngabe usuke ebona ilanga lihlehlela nyova yini okwemibono kaNongqawuse na? Ngabe usuke esesuthi yini nxa sihloniphisa elokudakwa? Ngabe usuke esekhohliwe yini yizinsuku lapho ayengenaye noyedwa umfazi na? Kunokwenzeka ukuthi sisuke sisilele noma esiziba ngamabomu esinye sezithako zensizi yezinsizi: ukwe'thembeka. Kunokwenzeka ukuthi esinye isithako siyakhumuzeka secwengeke kulensizi yezinsizi: Ukubonga. 
  Nxa ubonga usuke ulwa nokusuthisa umphefumulo uziqede umona nomhawu. Usuke ukhombisa ukuthi bakhona abangcono kunawe, akusiwena wedwa umuntu. Umuntu obongayo ngoba esizwa isidingo, nenhliziyo yakhe iyakhululeka. Obonga ngoba ezenzisa unanazela ngalamagama ekubongeni kwakhe: 'Kodwa ubungebe usangenzela kuthi xaxa? Ake uthi ukwengeza.' Lamazwi wena ophayo ahle akukhanyisele ukuthi usuwehlelwe ngokukhulu okuqeda ithumbu njengotshwala. 
  Eduzane nakwabo kaNomacala kwakungumuzi wamaKhaladi. Kwakukhona isalukazi esinguMaNdlovu esabe singugogo wazo zonke izingane zalapha ekhaya. Nokhoke zonke izingane isibongo sazo sabe sesaba nguOlifant. UNgcobo ekufikeni kwakhe eDumbe wayeqonywa laphaya ahlale khona, isikhashana usebonakala usengenise engxenye. Kwahamba kwahamba waze wangena lapha kwa-Olifant. Zazika kulomuzi izingxabo. Nakho-ke phela umfokazi lona wayenesondlo. Yilapha-ke elafika lavela khona igama lokuthi udukelene nezihlobo zakhe. 
  Lalidliwa iwayini kulomuzi. Kwakudliwa uhlobo olwabe lubizwa ngokuthi yi-sherry. UNgcobo wayesebenzile kakhulu ngazo zonke lezizinhlobo

  Wasala ezindla ngalendaba. Zabe sezomile izinyembezi. Wenza isinqumo esisha nemizindlo nomphefumulo wakhe. 'Lapho ekhona ngizomlanda. Sekungcono ngifele ukuthi into yami ngiyilandile. Kakade vele ezamasiso nxa zingafanga kufa umninizo.' Ngemva kwalemicabango wakhumbula ukukhuluma nabangabonwayo. Wacela amandla angatholwa kwabasathwabaza kulelizwe. Wayengaceli khona ukuthi angafi, kodwa wayecela ukuthi angazami ukubalekela ukufa ngoba kukhona yonke indawo, futhi kuyisiqhwaga esingahlehli. Wathandaza ecela ukuthi angabi ngumuntu onezinsolo nxa ubizo nenkonzo yakhe kulend~wo akuyo selufike esiphethweni. 
  Ngemva komkhuleko uThandi wathwebuleka. Waba namandla nophokophelo olusha, uphokophelo lokuhlenga ophule uSibeko. Wayeyenza lento ngemicabango. 'Ngoba kukhona abazingela impilo yami, kungcono ngiqinise impela ngoba lokho kusho ukuthi isikhathi siyanginciphela. Nxa ngiyeka manje ngesikhathi besasonga, ngiyolahlekelwa ngokuningi. Kunjani ngife ngilwa kunokuhti ngife ngibaleka? Ishinga aliyeki ukuba lishinga nxa bengekho abaqophisana balwe nalo balishaye. Nxa beqhamuka abalwa nalo, liyaye libe selicabanga ngaphambi kokuba liqhube ubulona balo. Ufuna ukungibulala? Sengifuna khona-ke ukufa ngoba kakho ozwela omunye ukuthi kunjani, futhi nxa ngifa ngingeke ngibuye ukuzoxoxela abantu.' 
  Sasesiside isikhathi izingane zihambile ziye kwaSishi. Naye wayesemehlwana ukuthi yini into ebambezele izingane zingasabuyi. Izingane nxa kukhona lapho ezisuke ziye khona ngokuvakasha ziye zingavamisi ukuthi qubasha zibe sezibuya. Lokhu kujwayelekile nxa zivakashele kwagogo. 
  Izingane zabafana zazithanda kakhulu ukuvakashela kwagogo wazo, Ezifundisweni. Igama las'Ezifundisweni babe sebelichumise laze lavuthwa. USibusiso wayengasayikhumbuli insotsha kayise. USikhumbuzo wayengamazi. Ngenxa yokuthi umuntu ogqoka ibhulukwe ezazimazi zonke izingane kwabe kungumkhulu wazo zazimkhonze kakhulu kabi. Nomkhulu ingane yomfana wayeyiqala ngabazukulu bakhe.

UThandi wake wacabanga ukumzekela indaba eyabe imehlele, kodwa wabuye wazikhuza. Izingane zamantombazane zabenzela itiye. Baphunga itiye lelo, bahlala isikhashana babe sebephelekezelana, ngoba nelanga labe selithambama.

  "Kulungile-ke ungahamba uyoqhubeka nomsebenzi wakho. Ngiyabona futhi ukuthi angizukukushintsha kulendawo okuyo ngoba ikhono lakho ngiyalithanda." Kusho uMalugqwayi. 
  Wahleka uNqobile ethokoziswa yilawomazwi okuthandeka kwekhono lakhe. 

  Wayezoshayisa ngensimbi yesine. Kwathi nxa lifika ihora lokuthi ashayise emsebenzini wabuyela kuMalugqwayi eyokuzwa ngesikhathi abemnike sona ngenkathi eva enkantolo. UMalugqwayi wamkhulula uku- " thi ashayise. Wahamba ebuyela ekhaya eyilokhu eyicabangela lemali. Wayecabanga ukuthi akhiphe umklomelo kumbe umvuzo kumuntu ongaba nokuthi akwazi ukunikeza umkhondo womyeni wakhe. Ecabanga ngokuthi enze inkonzo yesikhumbuzo somuntu owayeyisebenzile. Ecabanga ngomsebenzi wokulungisa itshe lesikhumbuzo likaDolothiya. Phela kwakungeyona imali kwakuyizisamasama. 

  Zaficana izinsuku kwaze kwafika osukwini Iwamanqamu 1010 ababelunqumele ukuya eHlobane. Bavuka bazilungiselela. Ngensimbi yesishiyagalombili babe sebesendleleni beyogibela uBantwanyana. UBantwanyana kwakuyisitimela, esabe sigcina khona eHlobane. Izimoto zazingakavami phela; noma zazikhona amatekisi aya eHlobane ayengekho. Banqamulela bayosigibelela eSikhame isitimela. Kwakulisonto lokugcina eseFilidi uMaNtuli. Kwasekuze kwaba yizikhathi ezintathu befika kwaNgenangesihle oSibeko noStutu bezobona uMaNtuli noKaMathenjwa. Nezingane zikaStutu zabe sezizazi njengezihlobo zazo izingane zakwaNgenangesihle. Lento yayibadida abantu abaningi. Babexakeka ukuthi uMaNtuli yini lena 
23 
emsanganisayo. 
  Phela ngokosiko Iwabantu abangazange bayazi noma abangakholelwa kuyo inhlambuluko enzulu, kwakufanele uMaNtuli alingise ikati egundaneni kuStutu. Wayengamelwe yikuthi aze abe nanobudlelwane obuyisilabi nje. Kodwa-ke uThandi wayencinda odengeleni Iwensizi yizinsizi, loludengele bonke ababencinda kulo babefika bakholwe ban came ukuthi yonke into umuntu ayenzayo ayibinayo impumelelo nxa ebuye ondle ancindise ubutha, Nxa umuntu enza ubutha kuwe, nawe ube usumenza isitha sakho, kusho ukuthi ubutha lobo uyabondla uyabukhuluphalisa. 
  Yinto eyayingamhluphi lena uThandiwe ngoba wayeseyenze waze wayenzisisa, wazijwayeza yona waze waphenduka waba yiyo, kabe esaba ngumenzi wayo. USibeko noStutu, bona babeyima bethwele itshe elizima, kuyilowo nalowo edliwa ngesakhe isazelo. Kwakukhona ukuziduduza kokuthi: "Qha ngoba usazoke ahambe angabikhona unyaka wonke ... " Kwakukhona nokungazethembi okwakusemizindlweni kokuthi: "Hhayi, usafihle induku emqubeni , .. " Nokho-ke noma yayisala ibe khona inhlansi eyabe iyilokhu ifiyofiyoza eyayifika ibavendleze yokuthi: "Kodwa kasenandaba nalutho uMaNtuli, unezimalimali usebenza umsebenzi' omuhle; uqondene nokusihlabekisa ... " 
  Izinto ezinjengalezi zihlale ziqhamuka yonke imihla. Siye sizibone izintombi nezinsizwa ezindleleni zobusha. Baqeda iminyaka abantu betha. ndana size sithi thina (sizibukelil: "Ngamandla angenawo umfo kabani, ngabe useyilobole ingane kabani: Kuyothi gwiqiqi simbone eseshada nentombi emqome ngesonto eledlule. Sesiphinda futhi siqhamuka sizibukeli nemibono yethu. Iqiniso lapha lisuke lilinye - sisuke sidukuza oswini 10' kungazi: Kodwa-ke, ayikho induku ebuhlungu njengenduku eshaya kungasali mvimbo namudwa; induku eshaya ikhathaze imizwa nomphefumulo. leso kusuke kuyisigwebo esilengisiwe. 
  Nomunye umuntu nxa ebekade ekwembela umgodi, awakhalakathela, kodwa wabe usumnika ithuba lokuba azisole asuke kulendawo abehleli kuyo uyaye agcwale ukungethembi ngenxa yokuthi ubelindele ukuthi wena uzolwa ngalendlela alwa ngayo, Omunye uze alimise ngesihloko elokuthi: 
"Kungcono ngingasizwa ngomunye hhayi lowo." Athi nokusho: "Yisitha sami Iowa."

ngasezukubuye bambone ngaphambi kokuthi aye phesheya. lolusuku baluchitha bekhuluma naye bebonisana ngokuthi yisiphi isivumelwano esisha abangase basenze. Babehlonga isivumelwano esingaba nokuthi sesule

  "Ngenza isinqumo baba kaMesuli. Angiseyena umuntu osebenza ngesivumelwano, ngoba sihlanganisa abantu ababili noma abangaphezu koyedwa. Sididiyela n6fakazi. Isinqumo yinto ekimi noqobo Iwami. Noma isingesinda isizima okwezigidigidi zesigidi, kodwa ngoba yinto ekimi eyaziwa yimi futhi eyenziwa yimi ngiyazi ukuthi ngeke ingehlule, Angiseyukubuye ngenze ezinye izifungo manje. Ngineqiniso ukuthi awekho adlula ukuthi: Isicelo sakho sentethelelo kimi nokuthayiza kukaStutu, ngakwamukela namanje ngisakwamukela." Kuqhubeka uThandiwe. 
  "Angisho ukuthi awukwamukeli. Kodwa ngiqonde ukuthi ngithole ukukhululeka emoyeni wami. Ngicela ungethule itshe elizima engazethwesa lona nokho manje esengixakeka yikuthi ngizozethula ndlelani. Umuntu onjalo ngumuntu ongeke nowayengeke awamukele amaqiniso okuthi kukhona into eyikuvivinywa ezweni okulandelwa yikuthi nxa umuntu ephuma kukho anxephezelwe ngokuphindaphindiwe. esembonile ukuthi uyameqhatha nezisebenzi zakhe, ithemba lakhe lamanga liphele. Umuntu ovamisa ukwazi yonke into uvamisa ukuba ngumuntu onamanga.    Nxa usebenza kumqashi umsebenzela kahle kodwa ungeneliswa yinkokhelo akunika yon a uthi nxa ezwa ukuthi usuthole umsebenzi ozokukhokhela kangcono, akonele phansi. Isimo esinjena, sidinga insizi yezinsizi. Eshumini lezinsizwa ezaliwa yizintombi zikade zithandana nazo ungathola ibe yinye engayithunazi iyilulaze intombi eyayalayo.   UNgcobo wayekuyo inkinga efana neyendoda efuna umsebenzi, kanti lapho yayikade iqashwe khona yayingawuyekanga kahle yayeqile. Wayesenkingeni yokufuna uthando Iwezingane zakhe. Wayesenkingeni yokufuna ukukholakala ezinganeni zakhe. Wayengakhohliwe yilokho okubusa abantu esiphila nabo lapha ezweni (Iabo abangenayo imiqondo ehluzekile nephefumulayo): 'Nxa webe kanye, ulisela. Ayikho into eyikuphenduka usuke ebubini uye ebuhleni.' Ujesu, sifunda eBhayibhelini ukuthi wathi kwabanye: 'Ongenasono kathathe itshe amkhande kuqala.' Wayefundisa ngendaba yothando uJesu. 
  Umuntu ongakancindi uyakhohlwa yikuthi lokho okuhle akutholayo, nabanye abaflhila lapha emhlabeni banelungelo lokuthi bakuthole. Ubuswa ngumona nomhawu. Ufuna ukuthethelelwa yena angathetheleli. Nxa ebuzwa umbuzo ngaye ukuthi: uzoze athethelelwe nje engafuni bathethelelwe abanye ngoba kunjani? Kufika kuhlale obala ukuthi udinga insizi yezinsizi.

Sibonga ukulunga Nanokubonelelwa Nokubukezelelwa Nkosi Wosibusisa. 

  Bathi bephakathi noNgeobo wayesesho ngembodlongo yakhe. Balingunga itafula kwayilowo nalowo waqondana nesitsha sakhe. Bathi bephakathi nokudla zehla kuSusana. Phela wayehlezi ebhekene noNgeobo. Kwathi nxa amehlo ehlangana kwathinteka .imizwa. Asazi-ke noma wayesuka abone umfanekiso wenkohliso noma wayekhaliswa yikuthi wamgeina ephila usehlangana naye ekulesisimo. 
  Nokho-ke wakuneenga ukudla uSusana. Phela kwasekwenzeka okwakuke kwenzeka kwabanye nokudeze kwenzeka, nxa ungakudli kuconselwa yizithukuthuku zakho ukudla kuconselwa yizinyembezi. Wayeyilokhu engazange awuvule umlomo wakhe uNgeobo. Wayezinika ithemba lokuthi uzosala ekhuluma naye ngomuso bengekho bonke abanye beye emsebenzini.
